< review>
My family was staying close by for a short vacation and we walked by Islander several times before we worked out a time to stop in. Now we are kicking ourselves that we didn't come sooner. The options you have when you come here are incredible. The quality of fish, the taste, and the overall experience are amazing. You cannot go wrong here (I personally recommend the lemon dill butter on grilled fish or the tempura fish and chips with horseradish tarter sauce).</review>

< Review>
It is a quaint little place, but their selection of fish is what brought me in. I had their fish & chips with Alaskan cod...best fish & chips I've had in the US. Neither needed anything put on them, but the plate included a double-horseradish tartar sauce that was awesome (avoid if you don't like horseradish though). Even though you order from a counter, the staff is friendly and really take care of you. I would definitely come here again.</Review>

<user>112399007076904054363<//user>< user_name>
Eric Sztanyo</user_name>
< Date>
1465358871870< /Date>
< rating>
5<//rating>
<Text>Friendly service. Yummy food. Awesome location.

Attending a seminar in San Diego, my wife and I had a brief lunch break. Look, we get to stare at the Ohio River all year. So, instead of hanging around the hotel and conference room any longer, we made a dash to Coronado.

Maybe it's not big deal for the locals, but us mid-westerners need to gobble up ocean views whenever we can!

And, we needed to gobble up some viddles. So, my wife pulls out Yelp on the way, and we the safe bet - go with the highest rated restaurant on Coronado ... there's a reason why.

It was Sunday afternoon. The weather wasn't great, a bit cloudy, so the Islander wasn't slammed. But, we were greeted by a wonderful hostess/waitress, who was extremely friendly. First, she told me I didn't need to pay the meter (which I had missed), then, she knew we were in a hurry and got our fish and chips order in right away. While it was getting ready, she prepped us to go with to go cups and the bill.

When the food came out, the chef (owner?), gave us a pro tip and said, "hey, it's fried. The sooner you open these styrofoam containers, the better it will be." Now, I should know that after years of takeout, but what a friendly and thoughtful tip! This guys was saying, "my food is really good. Here's how to get the most out of it if you are getting it to go."

And, it was delicious! The curry ketchup on the fries ... awesome! My wife hates ketchup, and she gobbled it all up. The horeradish tartar sauce, yum! The cod was fantastic and the pumpkin seed slaw great on the side.

A little pricey for what we normally pay ... but, that comes with the territory on Coronado. If you're going to pay premium, get the best. Go to the Islander!<//Text>< pics>
None<//pics>

None<//response>

< Text>
I have been a patient of Dr. Paisley's for over 10 years.  She has helped me through a high risk pregnancy, anxiety, panic attacks, hypothyroidism, adrenal gland fatigue, several really bad lower back muscle pulls, recovery from 8 major surgeries (including 2 brainstem surgeries in the last 2 years), fibromyalgia, and a chronic facial pain disorder called Trigeminal Neuralgia.  My husband has been treated by her a few times when he pulled his back out.  And I have been taking my kids to see her for maintenance adjustments about twice a year since they were 5 and 3 years old (they are now 12 and 10 years old).  I get adjustments from Dr. Paisley twice a month and I get a massage at least once a month from either Tim Knutson or Gretchen.  But really, ALL of the massage therapists at Paisley Wellness Center are awesome!  Each one has their own style and depending on what my body needs, the gals who do the scheduling, always book me with the massage therapist who style of massage is exactly what my body needs at the time.  I have also seen the in house Acupuncture lady and she is awesome too!  She is very knowledgeable about all of the different pressure points of the body, takes the time to explain it all to you, and is just really a cool person to talk to.  My go to massage therapist is Tim.  He is really a neat guy to talk to.  We often end up laughing and joking throughout my whole massage.  He is able to find all of the knots in my muscles and loosen them up.  And I like that he incorporates a good amount of stretching towards the end of my session.  Plus, he can usually accommodate my husbands work schedule so that I can get a massage in the evenings at 630pm when my husband can be home to watch the kids.

But Dr. Paisley is the main reason why I have been a loyal patient for over 10 years.  She is knowledgeable about naturopathic ways to help heal the body.  She sells and can recommend supplements, nutrients, and essential oils to help heal your body.  She offers electric stimulation for your muscles before your actual session with her.  She shows you exercises and stretches that you can do at home to help keep you spine and hips aligned.  She has even donated gift certificates for massage for different fundraisers that my family has been involved with.  All of those are awesome benefits of being her patient.  But there are three huge reasons why I am such a loyal patient of hers. 1) She actually reads your chart BEFORE your appointment so she knows what's going on and she keeps meticulous notes about your concerns, health issues, and the treatment/areas she adjusted during each appointment. 2) She actually gives you a REALLY good mini massage to loosen up the muscles around your spine and hips before she does the actual adjustment.  So she never has to do a hard "Snap, Crackle, Pop" neck twisting/pulling kind of adjustment.  By the time she is done massaging me, she barely has to move my head and neck to one side and my spine easily pops back into alignment.  And for my mid and lower back, after her mini massage, she usually just has to put a little pressure on the area, using her "Super Thumbs" as I call them, and my vertebrae just easily snaps back into place.  And did I mention the relaxing mini massage?  3) She does work with certain health insurance plans that offer chiropractic coverage.  And for those of us who don't have chiropractic insurance, she offers a money saving pre-paid program.  Actually there is a money saving prepaid program for chiropractic care and one for massage care.  With the massage program I can afford to get 2 90 minute massages month for what it would cost me to get
just one 60 minute massage at a day spa.

I HIGHLY recommend The Paisley Wellness Center in Poway.<//Text>

< Review>
Nice little 2-part park.  One end is a lush grassy area with bathrooms, basketball court and workout stations.  Other end is a little grassy area with lots of picnic ops and bathroom.  In between is either a walk along a busy road or a walk along the creek with lots of garbage, dog poop and discarded clothes.  Weird but I felt safe.  Some access to a little creek that's pretty stagnant in summer, but access areas are shady and trashed.< /Review>
